  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2245737187" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2245737187" />
    <a title="Kuroi Neko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/40503532-kuroi-neko"><img alt="Kuroi Neko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593341279p2/40503532.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2245737187?book_show_action=true">Jan 27, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kuroi Neko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kuroi Neko" href="/user/show/40503532-kuroi-neko">Kuroi Neko</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780998990927" href="/book/show/35926246-the-asylum-for-wayward-victorian-girls">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2245737187" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6359946811590502691">English/Italiano<br/>One of the best books I've ever read. I already loved Emilie Autumn as a singer, and now I am impressed by her writing abilities too.<br/>As usual, she's not scared to shock people by exposing the truth. And, in this book, the truth is that the line that divides the crazy people from the sane ones is really, really, thin. She explains how acts like self-harm and suicides are not something irrational, but there are valid reasons behind such actions, and society should start to understa</span>
  <span id="freeText6359946811590502691" style="display:none">English/Italiano<br />One of the best books I've ever read. I already loved Emilie Autumn as a singer, and now I am impressed by her writing abilities too.<br />As usual, she's not scared to shock people by exposing the truth. And, in this book, the truth is that the line that divides the crazy people from the sane ones is really, really, thin. She explains how acts like self-harm and suicides are not something irrational, but there are valid reasons behind such actions, and society should start to understand that, instead of simply labeling people as mentally ill and try to forget and hide their existence.<br /><br />I also enjoyed the historical/paranormal section of the novel. Every girl in the asylum is beautifully characterized, and I am sure I will remember them for a very long time. The ending was brilliant and breath-taking, I did not see it coming at all.<br /><br />In conclusion, this book is a roller-coaster inside inside the darkest part of the human mind.<br /><br /><b>ITALIANO</b><br /><br />Uno dei più bei libri io abbia mai letto. Ho sempre amato Emilie Aurtum come cantante, e adesso mi hanno impressionato anche le sue abilità come scrittrice.<br /><br />Come suo solito, Emilie Autumn non ha paura di turbare le persone evidenziando la realtà. In questo libro la scomoda realtà è che linea che separa le persone matte da quelle sane è molto, molto sottile. Spiega come l’autolesionismo, l’anoressia, il suicidio non siano atti irrazionali, ma spesso dietro ci sono delle valide ragioni per comportarsi in tale maniera. È questo che invita la società a capire, invece di etichettare le persone come “malate mentalmente” e provare a scordarsi della loro esistenza, e tavolta a nasconderle persino.<br /><br />Mi è piaciuta anche la parte storica e paranormale del romanzo. Ogni ragazza dell’asylum è caratterizzata in modo magistrale, e sono certa che mi rimaranno impresse nella mente per molto tempo. Il finale è stato brillante quanto il resto della storia, e mi ha lasciata senza fiato.<br /><br />In breve, questo romanzo è una montagna russa tra le parti più oscuri e interessanti della mente umana.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6359946811590502691" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_481015732" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/481015732" />
    <a title="Beth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15621959-beth"><img alt="Beth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1405456560p2/15621959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/481015732?book_show_action=true">Dec 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beth" href="/user/show/15621959-beth">Beth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15621959-beth?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer481015732" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16585276799910317954">This book is amazing, definitely on of my favourites. <br/>Not only is it amazing in terms of content it is also amazing visually (And I've always been a sucker for a beautiful book that looks good on the bookshelf)<br/><br/>The Asylum for Wayward Victorian Girls, is a semi-autobiographical, fantasy novel, I did think this to be an odd combination at first. However, Emilie Autumn presents the story in a way that works, with smooth changes from the real world to the fictional Asylum. <br/>This book is clearly very p</span>
  <span id="freeText16585276799910317954" style="display:none">This book is amazing, definitely on of my favourites. <br />Not only is it amazing in terms of content it is also amazing visually (And I've always been a sucker for a beautiful book that looks good on the bookshelf)<br /><br />The Asylum for Wayward Victorian Girls, is a semi-autobiographical, fantasy novel, I did think this to be an odd combination at first. However, Emilie Autumn presents the story in a way that works, with smooth changes from the real world to the fictional Asylum. <br />This book is clearly very personal the Emilie Autumn, it includes her Cutting Diary, Suicide Diary and Drug Diary. (MAY BE TRIGGERING) I admire the fact that she would share something so personal with her fans. <br /><br />Yes, this book is expensive but it's printed in full colour on high quality paper and you are, in a way, buying Emilie Autumn's diary. So in some ways the price can be justified. <br />If you are a fan of Emilie Autumn you should consider buying this book, if it were not for the price I would happily recommend this book to anyone.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16585276799910317954" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_149324910" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/149324910" />
    <a title="Dorian" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5007349-dorian"><img alt="Dorian" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564711805p2/5007349.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/149324910?book_show_action=true">Feb 19, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dorian" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dorian" href="/user/show/5007349-dorian">Dorian</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer149324910" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10968198914021409614">This book is one of my absolute favorites. It is amazingly written and has beautiful artwork in it as well. While partially a true story of Emilie's stay in a mental institution, there is a fictional story within about Emily (with a "y") who is staying in a Victorian Asylum. Having some of Emilie Autumn's actual handwriting in the book made it much more personal and made it seem much more like a journal than just any ordinary book. This is a must read for any "muffin" (Emilie Autumn fan).</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('MHO76lmzOf3nT/cCpYlec5QPc8b5WulLULPhajFU8ZaLaR9f0CeSIHj3+oW42vpQwMT9c/P07Tsf57h/tOzqOQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('a43Baq7QU+zANcne4Z1yFAJjsBTQU2xW1K3F9cBgQ+/Ql2XfJ0T4MV+NxFn8ztY3Vqg+odr9aCab+ZzgRdhYQA==')})
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/2528119.Emilie_Autumn">About Emilie Autumn</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/2528119.Emilie_Autumn"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1510961475p3/2528119.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/2528119.Emilie_Autumn">Emilie Autumn
</a></div>
<div class='goodreadsAuthorBadge'></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
1,220
followers
</div>

</div>
</div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer13237807587374315244">Emilie Autumn grew up by the sea in California where she mastered the classical violin before going on to travel the world as a singing theatrical performer and author. Globally known for her genre-bending album Fight Like A Girl, Emilie has also appeared as an actress, starring in Darren Lynn Bousman's musical fantasy films The Devil's Carnival and Alleluia! The Devil's Carnival.<br/><br/>Emilie’s academic</span>
  <span id="freeText13237807587374315244" style="display:none">Emilie Autumn grew up by the sea in California where she mastered the classical violin before going on to travel the world as a singing theatrical performer and author. Globally known for her genre-bending album Fight Like A Girl, Emilie has also appeared as an actress, starring in Darren Lynn Bousman's musical fantasy films The Devil's Carnival and Alleluia! The Devil's Carnival.<br /><br />Emilie’s academic career ended abruptly at the age of ten when she was removed from school to allow her the time to perfect her musical craft, yet, despite her near-complete absence of formal education, her debut self-published novel (the early editions of The Asylum for Wayward Victorian Girls) seems to demonstrate some understanding of proper spelling and grammar, and has been cited in text-books used as part of the psychology curriculum at Oxford University in London.<br /><br />Upon the release of her 2007 Shakespearean-themed concept album, Opheliac, Emilie found herself an overnight star in Germany's industrial rock scene, and began touring extensively. With her Victorian burlesque-themed stage show and signature heart painted on her cheek (a unifying symbol devotedly replicated by her international fan base known as "Plague Rats"), Emilie fast became a sensation throughout Europe and the United Kingdom before touring in America, South America, North America, and Russia.<br /><br />Diagnosed first with major depression in her early 20s and later with bipolar disorder, Emilie’s first novel (The Asylum…) was culled from the very real pages of the secret journal she kept whilst incarcerated in a mental hospital. She hopes that her future writings will not require such dramatic circumstances in order to be published.<br /><br />Since its fully-illustrated first edition hardcover release in 2008, The Asylum... continues to increase in popularity as Plague Rats around the globe cover themselves in tattoos from its elaborate art, cosplay as its eccentric characters (both human and animal), write their own fan-fiction, put on their own stage plays taking place in the "Asylum" world, arrange group tea party meet-ups, and incorporate Emilie's story into their own lives in virtually every imaginable way, beginning with the knowledge that what makes them different makes them magical and ought to be celebrated, not concealed.<br /><br />Emilie is presently composing and developing the Broadway musical and film versions of The Asylum for Wayward Victorian Girls. To follow her progress, join her on Twitter as @emilieautumn, on Instagram and Facebook as @emilieautumnofficial, and at her websites <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.emilieautumn.com">www.emilieautumn.com</a>, <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.theasylumforwaywardvictoriangirls.com">www.theasylumforwaywardvictoriangirls...</a>, and <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.theasylumemporium.com">www.theasylumemporium.com</a>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13237807587374315244" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>
